    <script>
        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set JohnGPT as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('johngpt')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Toggle create persona panel
            document.getElementById('create-persona-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-persona-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('persona-config-panel').classList.add('hidden');
            });
            
            document.getElementById('cancel-create').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-persona-panel').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('persona-config-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
            });
            
            // Color picker functionality
            const colorPickers = document.querySelectorAll('.grid.grid-cols-5 > div');
            colorPickers.forEach(picker => {
                picker.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    // Remove border from all
                    colorPickers.forEach(p => {
                        p.classList.remove('border-white');
                        p.classList.add('border-transparent');
                    });
                    // Add border to selected
                    this.classList.remove('border-transparent');
                    this.classList.add('border-white');
                });
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set JohnGPT as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('johngpt')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Toggle create prompt panel
            document.getElementById('create-prompt-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-prompt-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('prompt-config-panel').classList.add('hidden');
            });
            
            document.getElementById('cancel-create').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-prompt-panel').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('prompt-config-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
            });
            
            // Simulate token count animation
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.token-count').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = el.textContent.replace(/\d+/, () => {
                        return Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 150);
                    }) + ' tokens';
                });
            }, 500);
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set JohnGPT as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('johngpt')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Simulate token count animation
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.token-count').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = el.textContent.replace(/\d+/, () => {
                        return Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 200);
                    }) + ' tokens';
                });
            }, 500);
            
            // Save button functionality
            document.getElementById('save-prompt-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const originalText = this.innerHTML;
                this.innerHTML = '<svg class="animate-spin h-4 w-4 mr-2 inline text-white" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle><path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path></svg>Saving...';
                
                setTimeout(() => {
                    this.innerHTML = originalText;
                    alert('System prompt saved successfully! JohnGPT will reload with new configuration.');
                }, 1500);
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>

    <script>
        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set CMS as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('cms')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Toggle create slide panel
            document.getElementById('create-slide-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-slide-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('slide-config-panel').classList.add('hidden');
            });
            
            document.getElementById('cancel-create').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-slide-panel').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('slide-config-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
            });
            
            // Reordering functionality
            const reorderHandles = document.querySelectorAll('.reorder-handle');
            reorderHandles.forEach(handle => {
                handle.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
                    const item = this.closest('.p-3');
                    const container = item.parentElement;
                    
                    // Store original position
                    const startY = e.clientY;
                    const startRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
                    const startTop = startRect.top;
                    
                    // Create placeholder
                    const placeholder = document.createElement('div');
                    placeholder.className = 'border-2 border-dashed border-admin-red bg-admin-red/10 rounded-lg h-12 my-1';
                    container.insertBefore(placeholder, item);
                    
                    // Create ghost element
                    const ghost = item.cloneNode(true);
                    ghost.style.position = 'fixed';
                    ghost.style.top = `${startTop}px`;
                    ghost.style.left = `${startRect.left}px`;
                    ghost.style.width = `${startRect.width}px`;
                    ghost.style.zIndex = '1000';
                    ghost.style.opacity = '0.8';
                    document.body.appendChild(ghost);
                    
                    // Move ghost with cursor
                    const moveGhost = (e) => {
                        ghost.style.top = `${e.clientY - startRect.height / 2}px`;
                        ghost.style.left = `${e.clientX - startRect.width / 2}px`;
                        
                        // Check if we're hovering over another item
                        const items = container.querySelectorAll('.p-3');
                        for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                            const rect = items[i].getBoundingClientRect();
                            if (e.clientY < rect.top + rect.height / 2) {
                                container.insertBefore(placeholder, items[i]);
                                break;
                            }
                            if (i === items.length - 1) {
                                container.appendChild(placeholder);
                            }
                        }
                    };
                    
                    // Mouse move handler
                    const mouseMove = (e) => {
                        moveGhost(e);
                    };
                    
                    // Mouse up handler
                    const mouseUp = () => {
                        // Remove event listeners
                        document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMove);
                        document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUp);
                        
                        // Move original item to new position
                        container.insertBefore(item, placeholder);
                        
                        // Clean up
                        document.body.removeChild(ghost);
                        placeholder.remove();
                        
                        // Update sort order numbers
                        const items = container.querySelectorAll('.p-3');
                        items.forEach((item, index) => {
                            const span = item.querySelector('span');
                            if (span) {
                                span.textContent = `Order #${index + 1}`;
                            }
                        });
                    };
                    
                    // Add event listeners
                    document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMove);
                    document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUp);
                });
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set Feature Flags as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('feature-flags')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Toggle create feature panel
            document.getElementById('create-feature-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-feature-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('feature-config-panel').classList.add('hidden');
            });
            
            document.getElementById('cancel-create').addEventListener('click', function() {
                document.getElementById('create-feature-panel').classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById('feature-config-panel').classList.remove('hidden');
            });
        });
    </script>

        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set Migration Center as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('migration-center')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Simulate progress bars for demo
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.progress-value').forEach(bar => {
                    const width = bar.style.width;
                    bar.style.width = '0%';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        bar.style.width = width;
                    }, 200);
                });
            }, 300);
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        // Auto-apply theme
        if (localStorage.theme === 'dark' || (!('theme' in localStorage) && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches)) {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')
        }
        
        // Initialize sidebar active state
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Set System Diagnostics as active in sidebar
            const sidebarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item');
            sidebarItems.forEach(item => {
                if (item.href.includes('system-diagnostic')) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            // Simulate progress bars for demo
            setTimeout(() => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.progress-value').forEach(bar => {
                    const width = bar.style.width;
                    bar.style.width = '0%';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        bar.style.width = width;
                    }, 200);
                });
            }, 300);
        });
    </script>
